date: "2018-07-05"
categories: type-theory

---

This is my attempt to collect in just one-file, a basic overview of HoTT in Agda.
This source code was type-checked by Agda 2.5.4.

Based on:

<div class="references" markdown="1">
- https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/
- https://mroman42.github.io/ctlc/agda-hott/Total.html
</div>

Agda has a pragma to work with HoTT (`--without-K`):

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="455" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="459" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="467" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="479" class="Symbol">#-}</a>
<a id="483" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="488" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="495" href="Agda.Primitive.html" class="Module">Agda.Primitive</a> <a id="510" class="Keyword">public</a>

<a id="518" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#518" class="Function">_</a> <a id="520" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="522" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="526" class="Comment">-- trick for avoiding Agda module errors (jekyll)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Universes
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type universe hierarchy. It hides Agda primitive
hierarchy and the keyword `Set`. It uses `Type` instead.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="799" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Universes"></a><a id="806" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#806" class="Module">Universes</a> <a id="816" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="825" class="Comment">-- Our Universe hierarchy. It is implemented over the primitive</a>
  <a id="891" class="Comment">-- Agda universe hierarchy but it uses Type instead of Set, the</a>
  <a id="957" class="Comment">-- usual name for the Universe in Agda.</a>

Types
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Empty Type

The empty type, representing falsehood.

<a id="1525" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="⊥"></a><a id="1530" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1530" class="Datatype">⊥</a> <a id="1532" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1533" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1533" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="1535" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="1537" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1539" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="1544" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1533" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="1547" class="Keyword">where</a>

### Unit

The unit type is defined as record so that we also get the η-rule definitionally.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="1860" class="Comment">-- A record without fields is the unit type with a single</a>
<a id="1918" class="Comment">-- constructor.</a>
<a id="1934" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="⊤"></a><a id="1941" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1941" class="Record">⊤</a> <a id="1943" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1945" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1097" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="1951" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="1959" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="⊤.★"></a><a id="1971" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1971" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>

<a id="unit"></a><a id="1974" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1974" class="Function">unit</a> <a id="1979" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1981" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1971" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>

<a id="1984" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="1988" class="Keyword">BUILTIN</a> UNIT <a id="2001" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1941" class="Record">⊤</a> <a id="2003" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Basic types of Martin-Löf type theory and some basic
functions.

### Σ-types

Sigma types are a particular case of records, but records can be
constructed using only sigma types. Note that l ⊔ q is the maximum
of two hierarchy levels l and q. This way, we define sigma types in
full generality, at each universe.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2346" class="Keyword">infixr</a> <a id="2353" class="Number">60</a> <a id="2356" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2445" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>
<a id="2360" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="Σ"></a><a id="2367" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2367" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="2369" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2370" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2370" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="2373" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2373" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="2375" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2377" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2378" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2378" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="2380" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2382" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="2387" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2370" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="2389" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="2391" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2391" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="2393" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2395" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2378" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="2397" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2399" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="2404" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2373" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="2406" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2408" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2410" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="2415" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2416" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2370" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="2419" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="2421" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2373" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="2423" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2425" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="2433" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="Σ._,_"></a><a id="2445" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2445" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>
  <a id="2451" class="Keyword">field</a>
    <a id="Σ.fst"></a><a id="2461" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2461" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="2465" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2467" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2378" class="Bound">S</a>

<a id="2485" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="2490" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2367" class="Module">Σ</a> <a id="2492" class="Keyword">public</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### Products (×)

Product type as a particular case of the sigma

### Boolean

Boolean type, two constants true and false

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3099" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Bool"></a><a id="3104" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3104" class="Datatype">Bool</a> <a id="3109" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3111" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1097" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="3117" class="Keyword">where</a>

* Booleans can be defined by using a coproduct.

### Natural numbers

Natural numbers are the initial algebra for a constant and a
successor function. The BUILTIN declaration allows us to use
natural numbers in arabic notation.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3407" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="ℕ"></a><a id="3412" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3414" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3416" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1097" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="3422" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="ℕ.zero"></a><a id="3430" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3430" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a> <a id="3435" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3437" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
  <a id="ℕ.succ"></a><a id="3441" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3441" class="InductiveConstructor">succ</a> <a id="3446" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3448" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3450" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3452" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

<a id="Nat"></a><a id="3455" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3455" class="Function">Nat</a> <a id="3459" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3461" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

<a id="3464" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="3468" class="Keyword">BUILTIN</a> NATURAL <a id="3484" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3486" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


### Common functions

#### Identity function
The identity function with implicit type.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="id"></a><a id="3603" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3603" class="Function">id</a> <a id="3606" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3608" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="3610" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3611" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3611" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="3612" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3614" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3615" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3615" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3617" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3619" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="3624" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3611" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="3625" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3627" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3629" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3615" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3631" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3633" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3615" class="Bound">A</a>

The identity function on a type `A` is `idf A`.

some errors for my jekyll configuration.

#### Instance Searh

### Identity Type

Equality is defined as an inductive type. Its induction principle
is the J-eliminator.

### PathOver

If you have a dependent type `B` over `A`, a path `p : x == y` in `A` and two
points `u : B x` and `v : B y`, there is a **type** `[u == v [ B ↓ p]]` of paths
from `u` to `v` lying over the path `p`.  By definition, if `p` is a constant
path, then `[u == v [ B ↓ p ]]` is just an ordinary path in the fiber.
[More info here](https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/blob/master/core/lib/Base.agda#L115).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="PathOver"></a><a id="6346" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6346" class="Function">PathOver</a> <a id="6355" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6357" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="6359" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6360" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6360" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="6363" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6363" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="6365" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6367" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6368" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6368" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6370" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6372" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="6377" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6360" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="6379" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6381" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6382" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6382" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="6384" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6386" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6368" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6388" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6390" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="6395" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6363" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="6397" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="6502" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="6508" class="Number">30</a> <a id="6511" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6346" class="Function">PathOver</a>
<a id="6520" class="Keyword">syntax</a> <a id="6527" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6346" class="Function">PathOver</a> B p u v <a id="6544" class="Symbol">=</a> u == v [ B ↓ p ]{% endraw %}</pre>

## Equational Reasoning

Equational reasoning is a way to write readable chains of equalities.
The idea is that you can write the following:

{% raw %}
```agda
  t : a == e
  t = a =⟨ p ⟩
      b =⟨ q ⟩
      c =⟨ r ⟩
      d =⟨ s ⟩
      e ∎
```
{% endraw %}

where `p` is a path from `a` to `b`, `q` is a path from `b` to `c`, and so on.
You often have to apply some equality in some context, for instance `p` could be
`ap ctx thm` where `thm` is the interesting theorem used to prove that `a` is
equal to `b`, and `ctx` is the context. [More info here](https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/blob/master/core/lib/Base.agda#L270).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="7218" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="EquationalReasoning"></a><a id="7225" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7225" class="Module">EquationalReasoning</a> <a id="7245" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7246" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7246" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="7248" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7250" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7251" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7251" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7253" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7255" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="7260" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7246" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="7262" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7264" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="7273" class="Comment">-- Common combinators for equational reasoning. They allow us to</a>
  <a id="7340" class="Comment">-- write proof in an equational style. These versions have been</a>
  <a id="7406" class="Comment">-- adapted from the old version of the HoTT-agda library.</a>

<a id="7770" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="7775" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7225" class="Module">EquationalReasoning</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Actions on paths I

Properties and structure of the equality type.

### Equality

Types are higher groupoids.  If we see equalities as paths, this
is the inverse of a path. If we see equalities classically, this
is the symmetric property of equality.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="inv"></a><a id="8074" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8074" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="8078" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8080" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="8082" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8082" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="8083" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8085" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8086" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8086" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8088" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8090" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="8095" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8082" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="8096" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="8099" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8100" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8100" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8102" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8102" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="8104" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8106" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8086" class="Bound">A</a><a id="8107" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="8111" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8113" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8100" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8115" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5183" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8118" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8102" class="Bound">b</a>
  <a id="8122" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8124" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8102" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="8126" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5183" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8129" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8100" class="Bound">a</a>
<a id="8131" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8074" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="8135" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8136" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5230" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="8141" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8141" class="Bound">a</a><a id="8142" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8144" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8146" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5230" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="8151" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8141" class="Bound">a</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
Functions are functors to equalities.  In other words, functions
preserve equalities.

## Properties on the groupoid

<a id="9855" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="9860" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8960" class="Module">·-Properties</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Transport

When we transport a proof of `(P a)` over an equality `(a == b)`, we
get a proof of `(P b)`.

                <a id="14227" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14229" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14230" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14230" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="14232" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14234" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14166" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14236" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5183" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14239" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14168" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14240" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14242" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14244" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14245" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14245" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14247" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14249" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14176" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14251" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14166" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14253" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14255" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14194" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14257" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14166" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14258" class="Symbol">)</a>

## Homotopy

In a type-theoretical sense, a homotopy between two
functions is a family of equalities between their applications.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14715" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Homotopy"></a><a id="14722" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14722" class="Module">Homotopy</a> <a id="14731" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14732" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14732" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="14735" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14735" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14737" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14739" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14740" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14740" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14742" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14744" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14749" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14732" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="14751" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14753" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14754" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14754" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="14756" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14758" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14740" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14760" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14762" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14767" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14735" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14769" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14771" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="14779" class="Comment">-- A homotopy is a natural isomorphism between two functions, we will write</a>
  <a id="14857" class="Comment">-- f ∼ g when (f x == g x) for all x.</a>
  <a id="Homotopy.homotopy"></a><a id="14897" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14897" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="14906" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14908" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14909" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14909" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14911" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14911" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14913" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14915" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14917" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14917" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14919" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14921" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14740" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14922" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14924" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14926" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14754" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="14928" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14917" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14929" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="14932" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14934" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14939" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14940" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14732" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="14943" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="14945" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14735" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14947" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="14951" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14897" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="14960" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14960" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14962" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14962" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14964" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14966" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14967" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14967" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14969" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14971" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14740" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14972" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14974" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14976" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14960" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14978" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14967" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14980" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5183" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14983" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14962" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14985" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14967" class="Bound">x</a>

  <a id="Homotopy._∼_"></a><a id="14990" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14990" class="Function Operator">_∼_</a> <a id="14994" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14996" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14997" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14997" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14999" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14999" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="15001" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15003" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="15005" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15005" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15007" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15009" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14740" class="Bound">A</a><a id="15010" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15012" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15014" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14754" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="15016" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15005" class="Bound">x</a><a id="15017" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="15020" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15022" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="15027" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15028" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14732" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="15031" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="15033" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14735" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="15035" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="15039" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15039" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15041" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14990" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="15043" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15043" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="15045" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15047" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14897" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="15056" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15039" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15058" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15043" class="Bound">g</a>

  <a id="15063" class="Comment">-- Homotopy is an equivalence relation</a>
  <a id="Homotopy.h-refl"></a><a id="15104" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15104" class="Function">h-refl</a> <a id="15111" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15113" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15114" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15114" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15116" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15118" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15119" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15119" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15121" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15123" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14740" class="Bound">A</a><a id="15124" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15126" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15128" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14754" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="15130" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15119" class="Bound">x</a><a id="15131" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15133" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15135" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15114" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15137" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14990" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="15139" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15114" class="Bound">f</a>

## Naturality

Homotopy is natural, meaning that it satisfies the following
square commutative diagram.

A particular case of naturality on the identity function.

## Contractible types

## Equivalence

    <a id="18344" class="Comment">-- Contractible maps. A map is contractible if the fiber in any</a>
    <a id="18412" class="Comment">-- point is contractible, that is, each element has a unique</a>
    <a id="18477" class="Comment">-- preimage.</a>
    <a id="Equivalence.DefinitionOfEquivalence.isContrMap"></a><a id="18494" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18494" class="Function">isContrMap</a> <a id="18505" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18507" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18508" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18508" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18510" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18512" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18307" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18514" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18516" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18321" class="Bound">B</a><a id="18517" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18519" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18521" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="18526" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18527" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18299" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="18530" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="18532" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18302" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="18534" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="18588" class="Comment">-- There exists an equivalence between two types if there exists a</a>
    <a id="18659" class="Comment">-- contractible function between them.</a>

## Cartesian Product

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="22011" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="CartesianProduct"></a><a id="22018" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22018" class="Module">CartesianProduct</a> <a id="22035" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22036" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22036" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="22039" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22039" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="22041" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22043" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22044" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22044" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="22046" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22048" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="22053" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22036" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="22055" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22057" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22058" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22058" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="22060" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22062" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="22067" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22039" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="22069" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22071" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="22080" class="Comment">-- In a pair, the equality of the two components of the pairs is</a>
  <a id="22147" class="Comment">-- equivalent to equality of the two pairs.</a>
  <a id="CartesianProduct.prodComponentwise"></a><a id="22193" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22193" class="Function">prodComponentwise</a> <a id="22211" <a id="22925" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="22930" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22018" class="Module">CartesianProduct</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## DecidableEquality

A type has decidable equality if any two of its
elements are equal or different. This would be a particular
instance of the Law of Excluded Middle that holds even if we do not
assume Excluded Middle.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="23196" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="DecidableEquality"></a><a id="23203" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23203" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a> <a id="23221" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23222" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23222" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="23223" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23225" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="23234" class="Comment">-- A type has decidable equality if we can prove that any two of its</a>
  <a id="23305" class="Comment">-- elements are equal or different.</a>
  <a id="DecidableEquality.decEq"></a><a id="23343" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23343" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="23349" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23351" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23352" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23352" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23354" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23356" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="23361" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23222" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="23362" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23364" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23366" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="23371" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23222" class="Bound">ℓ</a>
  <a id="23375" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23343" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="23381" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23381" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23383" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23385" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23386" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23386" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="23388" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23388" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="23390" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23392" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23381" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23393" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23395" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23397" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23398" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23386" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="23400" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5183" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="23403" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23388" class="Bound">b</a><a id="23404" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23406" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2918" class="Datatype Operator">+</a> <a id="23408" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1692" class="Function">¬</a> <a id="23410" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23411" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23386" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="23413" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5183" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="23416" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23388" class="Bound">b</a><a id="23417" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="23422" class="Comment">-- The product of types with decidable equality is a type with</a>
  <a id="23487" class="Comment">-- decidable equality.</a>

<a id="23908" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="23913" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23203" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Propositions

Propositions as described on the main text. A type
is a proposition if we can create a function making any two of its
elements equal. We create a type of propositions.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="24143" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Propositions"></a><a id="24150" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24150" class="Module">Propositions</a> <a id="24163" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="24172" class="Comment">-- A type is a mere proposition if any two inhabitants of the type</a>
  <a id="24241" class="Comment">-- are equal</a>
  <a id="Propositions.isProp"></a><a id="24256" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24256" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24263" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24265" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24267" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24267" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24268" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="24271" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24272" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24272" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24274" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24276" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24281" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24267" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24282" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24284" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24286" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24291" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24267" class="Bound">ℓ</a>
  <a id="24295" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24256" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24302" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24302" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24304" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24306" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24308" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24308" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24310" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24310" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="24312" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24314" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24302" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24315" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24317" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24319" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24308" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24321" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5183" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="24324" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24310" class="Bound">y</a><a id="24325" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="24330" class="Comment">-- The type of mere propositions</a>
  <a id="Propositions.hProp"></a><a id="24365" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24365" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="24371" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24373" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24375" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24375" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24376" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24378" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24380" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24385" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24386" href="Agda.Primitive.html#627" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="24391" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24375" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24392" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24396" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24365" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="24402" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24403" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24403" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24404" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24406" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24408" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2367" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="24410" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24411" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24416" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24403" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24417" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24419" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24256" class="Function">isProp</a>


  <a id="24430" class="Comment">-- The dependent function type to proposition types is itself a</a>
  <a id="24496" class="Comment">-- proposition.</a>
  <a id="Propositions.piProp"></a><a id="24514" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24514" class="Function">piProp</a> <a id="24521" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24523" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24525" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24525" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="24528" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24528" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24530" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24532" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24534" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24535" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24535" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24537" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24539" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24544" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24525" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="24546" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24548" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24550" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24551" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24551" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24553" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24555" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24535" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24557" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24559" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24564" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24528" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24566" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="24577" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24579" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24581" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24581" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24583" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24585" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24535" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24586" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24588" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24590" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24256" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24597" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24598" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24551" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24600" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24581" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24601" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="24604" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24606" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24256" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24613" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24615" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24615" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24617" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24619" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24535" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24620" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24622" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24624" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24551" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24626" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24615" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24627" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24631" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24514" class="Function">piProp</a> <a id="24638" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24638" class="Bound">props</a> <a id="24644" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24644" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="24646" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24646" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="24648" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24650" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20341" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="24657" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="24659" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24659" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24661" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24663" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24638" class="Bound">props</a> <a id="24669" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24659" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24671" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24672" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24644" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="24674" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24659" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24675" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24677" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24678" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24646" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="24680" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24659" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24681" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="24686" class="Comment">-- The product of propositions is itself a proposition.</a>
  <a id="Propositions.isProp-prod"></a><a id="24744" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24744" class="Function">isProp-prod</a> <a id="24756" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24758" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24760" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24760" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="24763" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24763" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24765" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24767" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24769" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24770" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24770" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24772" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24774" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24779" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24760" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="24781" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24783" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24785" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24786" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24786" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24788" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24790" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24795" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24763" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24797" class="Symbol">}</a>
              <a id="24813" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24815" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24256" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24822" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24770" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24824" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24826" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24256" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24833" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24786" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24835" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24837" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24256" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24844" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24845" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24770" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24847" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2743" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="24849" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24786" class="Bound">B</a><a id="24850" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="24914" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="24919" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24150" class="Module">Propositions</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Sets

Sets are types without any higher dimensional structure, all
parallel paths are homotopic and the homotopy is given by a
continuous function on the two paths.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="25127" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Sets"></a><a id="25134" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25134" class="Module">Sets</a> <a id="25139" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="25148" class="Comment">-- A type is a &quot;set&quot; by definition if any two equalities on the type</a>
  <a id="25219" class="Comment">-- are equal.</a>

<a id="25834" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="25839" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25134" class="Module">Sets</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## HLevels

Higher levels of the homotopical structure, where the
first levels are:

- Contractible types (0)
- Propositions (1)
- Sets (2)

They would correspond to homotopy levels. We only work with
these first levels.

## EquivalenceProp

Equivalence of two types is a proposition
Moreover, equivalences preserve propositions.

<a id="28102" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="28107" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#27320" class="Module">EquivalenceProp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Half-Adjoints

Half-adjoints are an auxiliary notion that helps us
to define a suitable notion of equivalence, meaning that it is a
proposition and that it captures the usual notion of equivalence.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="28351" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Halfadjoints"></a><a id="28358" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28358" class="Module">Halfadjoints</a> <a id="28371" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28372" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28372" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="28375" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28375" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28377" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28379" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28380" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28380" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28382" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28384" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28389" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28372" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="28391" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28393" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28394" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28394" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="28396" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28398" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28403" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28375" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28405" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28407" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="28416" class="Comment">-- Half adjoint equivalence.</a>
  <a id="28447" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="Halfadjoints.ishae"></a><a id="28454" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28454" class="Record">ishae</a> <a id="28460" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28461" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28461" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="28463" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28465" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28380" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28467" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28469" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28394" class="Bound">B</a><a id="28470" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28472" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28474" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28479" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28480" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28372" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="28483" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="28485" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28375" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28487" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28489" class="Keyword">where</a>

## Quasiinverses

Two functions are quasiinverses if we can construct
a function providing gfx = x and fgy = y for any given x and y.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="31208" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Quasiinverses"></a><a id="31215" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31215" class="Module">Quasiinverses</a> <a id="31229" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31230" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31230" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="31233" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31233" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="31235" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31237" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31238" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31238" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="31240" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31242" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="31247" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31230" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="31249" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31251" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31252" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31252" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="31254" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31256" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="31261" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31233" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="31263" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31265" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="33961" class="Comment">-- Half-adjoint equivalences are quasiinverses.</a>

     <a id="35425" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2461" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="35429" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35430" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35038" class="Function">invEqv</a> <a id="35437" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35352" class="Bound">α</a><a id="35438" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35440" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4075" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="35442" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2461" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="35446" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35352" class="Bound">α</a>     <a id="35452" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7563" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="35456" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20341" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="35463" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35464" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19610" class="Function">rlmap-inverse-h</a> <a id="35480" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35352" class="Bound">α</a><a id="35481" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35483" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7563" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
     <a id="35490" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3603" class="Function">id</a>
   <a id="35496" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7662" class="Function Operator">∎</a><a id="35497" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="35500" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="35505" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#34246" class="Module">EquivalenceComposition</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Univalence

Voevodsky's univalence axiom is postulated. It induces
an equality between any two equivalent types. Some β and η rules
are provided.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="35704" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Univalence"></a><a id="35711" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35711" class="Module">Univalence</a> <a id="35722" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="35766" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="UnivalenceAxiom"></a><a id="35773" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35773" class="Module">UnivalenceAxiom</a> <a id="35789" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35790" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35790" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="35791" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35793" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35794" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35794" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="35796" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35796" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="35798" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35800" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="35805" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35790" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="35806" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35808" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="36508" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="36513" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35773" class="Module">UnivalenceAxiom</a> <a id="36529" class="Keyword">public</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Somme lemmas about Univelance

{: .foldable}
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="36607" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36610" class="Comment">--   module UnivalenceLemmas {ℓ} where</a>
<a id="36649" class="Comment">--     -- The identity equivalence creates the trivial path.</a>
<a id="36710" class="Comment">--     ua-id : {A : Type ℓ} → ua idEqv == refl A</a>
<a id="36759" class="Comment">--     ua-id {A} =</a>
<a id="36778" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="36793" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv              ==⟨ ap ua (sameEqv (refl id)) ⟩</a>
<a id="36858" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (refl A)) ==⟨ ua-η (refl A) ⟩</a>
<a id="36911" class="Comment">--         refl A</a>
<a id="36929" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="36940" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36943" class="Comment">--     -- The composition of equivalences is preserved into composition</a>
<a id="37015" class="Comment">--     -- of equalities.</a>
<a id="37040" class="Comment">--     ua-comp : {A B C : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → (β : B ≃ C) → ua (compEqv α β) == ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="37136" class="Comment">--     ua-comp α β =</a>
<a id="37157" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="37172" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α β)                               ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv x β)) (inv (ua-β α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="37279" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) β)                ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) x))</a>
<a id="37384" class="Comment">--                                                            (inv (ua-β β)) ⟩</a>
<a id="37463" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β))) ==⟨ ap ua lemma ⟩</a>
<a id="37539" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))                     ==⟨ ua-η (ua α · ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="37622" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="37645" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="37656" class="Comment">--       where</a>
<a id="37671" class="Comment">--         lemma : compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β)) == idtoeqv (ua α · ua β)</a>
<a id="37757" class="Comment">--         lemma = sameEqv (</a>
<a id="37786" class="Comment">--           begin</a>
<a id="37805" class="Comment">--             fst (idtoeqv (ua β)) ∘ fst (idtoeqv (ua α))                 ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="37893" class="Comment">--             (transport (λ x → x) (ua β)) ∘ (transport (λ x → x) (ua α)) ==⟨ transport-comp (ua α) (ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="38003" class="Comment">--             transport (λ x → x) (ua α · ua β)                           ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="38091" class="Comment">--             fst (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))</a>
<a id="38134" class="Comment">--           ∎)</a>
<a id="38150" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="38153" class="Comment">--     -- Inverses are preserved.</a>
<a id="38187" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua α · ua (invEqv α) == refl A</a>
<a id="38267" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r α =</a>
<a id="38287" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="38302" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua (invEqv α)      ==⟨ inv (ua-comp α (invEqv α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="38372" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α (invEqv α)) ==⟨ ap ua (compEqv-inv α) ⟩</a>
<a id="38437" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv                  ==⟨ ua-id ⟩</a>
<a id="38486" class="Comment">--         refl _</a>
<a id="38504" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>

<a id="38518" class="Comment">--     ua-inv : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua (invEqv α) == inv (ua α)</a>
